<hr>
<h2>2. Codex host <code>web_search</code> delegation</h2>
<h3>Config generator preserves user flag</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// src/config/__tests__/generator-notify.test.ts:237-259
const existing = [
  'model = "o3"',
  '[features]',
  'web_search = true',
].join('\n');
await mergeConfig(configPath, wd);
// assert: web_search = true still present after OMX merge
</code></pre>
<p>OMX <code>mergeConfig</code> <strong>adds</strong> OMX keys (<code>notify</code>, <code>multi_agent</code>, <code>goals</code>) without clobbering existing <code>web_search</code> feature flag.</p>
<h3>What <code>web_search = true</code> activates</h3>
<p>See <code>014_web-search/14_co_web-search.md</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Rust <code>ToolSpec::WebSearch</code> in <code>codex-rs/tools/src/tool_spec.rs</code></li>
<li>Modes <code>live</code> / <code>cached</code> / <code>disabled</code> via <code>~/.codex/config.toml</code></li>
<li>OpenAI Responses server pipeline (Bing + OAI-SearchBot + rerank)</li>
</ul>
<p>OMX does not ship Rust sources — it only ensures Codex config allows the host tool.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Researcher agent prompt (methodology layer)</h2>
<p><code>171_oh-my-codex/prompts/researcher.md</code> defines external research behavior:</p>
<pre><code class="language-markdown">// :73-76 (tools section)
Use web search/fetch for official docs, versioned references, release notes...
Use Context7 MCP for resolved library IDs when registered; fall back to web search otherwise.
</code></pre>
<h3>Repo research surface (<code>:40-48</code>)</h3>
<ul>
<li><code>gh search code</code>, <code>gh search repos</code> for OSS discovery</li>
<li>Pinned SHA raw URLs: <code>https://raw.githubusercontent.com/&#x3C;org>/&#x3C;repo>/&#x3C;sha>/&#x3C;path></code></li>
<li>Context7 when <code>omx setup</code> registered MCP</li>
<li>Citation format: <code>org/repo@sha:path:Lx-Ly</code></li>
</ul>
<p>This is <strong>prompt contract only</strong> — execution requires Codex <code>web_search</code> enabled and/or MCP servers configured by user/<code>omx setup</code>.</p>

<hr>
<h2>5. Historical note: <code>$research</code> removal</h2>
<p><code>CHANGELOG.md</code> (~line 1779 in corpus) documents <code>$research</code> skill removal in favor of <code>$external-context</code> for web searches — OMX moved research orchestration from a single skill token to explicit agent roles + host tools.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. <code>omx_wiki</code> vs internet search</h2>
<p><code>omx_wiki</code> MCP (<code>wiki-server.js</code>) stores <strong>persistent project knowledge</strong> accumulated during OMX sessions — architecture notes, decisions, glossary. It does not fetch URLs.</p>
<p>Recommended division:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Internet / official docs</strong> → Codex <code>web_search</code> + <code>WebFetch</code> (host) + optional Context7 MCP</li>
<li><strong>Project-specific recall</strong> → <code>omx_wiki</code> + <code>omx_memory</code></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>7. Code intelligence as search substitute</h2>
<p><code>omx_code_intel</code> provides LSP diagnostics and AST-grep style search <strong>within the workspace</strong>. Useful for "find pattern in repo" queries that would be wrong to send to <code>web_search</code>.</p>
<p>Contrast OMO's <code>grep_app</code> which searches <strong>public GitHub</strong> via remote MCP.</p>
<hr>
<h2>8. Hermes coordination MCP</h2>
<p><code>omx_hermes</code> can dispatch worker agents (including researcher role) but does not implement search itself — workers inherit host <code>web_search</code> availability from generated <code>config.toml</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>9. Setup path for full web research stack</h2>
<p>Typical OMX operator configuration:</p>
<ol>
<li><code>omx setup</code> / <code>mergeConfig</code> — preserve or set <code>web_search = true</code> under <code>[features]</code></li>
<li>Register Context7 MCP manually if desired (not in first-party six)</li>
<li>Use <code>researcher</code> agent for docs-first external queries</li>
<li>Use <code>explore</code> agent for repo-local code (not web)</li>
</ol>

<h2>12. <code>omx_wiki</code> MCP tools (local, not web)</h2>
<p><code>wiki-server.ts</code> exposes tools such as <code>queryWiki</code>, <code>readPage</code>, <code>ingestKnowledge</code>, <code>listPages</code> (<code>:10-23</code>, <code>buildWikiServerTools</code> <code>:60+</code>).</p>
<p>Categories: <code>architecture</code>, <code>decision</code>, <code>pattern</code>, <code>debugging</code>, <code>environment</code>, <code>session-log</code>, <code>reference</code>, <code>convention</code> (<code>:32-41</code>).</p>
<p><strong>Not a substitute for <code>web_search</code>:</strong> wiki ingests session knowledge to disk under project state paths (<code>resolveWorkingDirectoryForState</code> <code>:54-57</code>). Internet facts belong in Codex host search, then optionally <code>ingestKnowledge</code> to wiki for retention.</p>
<hr>
<h2>13. Config generator behavior (extended)</h2>
<p>Beyond preserving <code>web_search = true</code>, OMX generator adds:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>notify</code> hooks array</li>
<li><code>model_reasoning_effort</code></li>
<li><code>[agents] max_threads = 6</code>, <code>max_depth = 2</code> (<code>generator-notify.test.ts:269-278</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>None of these OMX-specific keys implement search — they shape agent parallelism for research workloads.</p>
<hr>
<h2>14. External Context7 registration</h2>
<p>Researcher prompt references Context7 "when registered via <code>omx setup</code>" (<code>researcher.md:46</code>). Context7 is <strong>not</strong> in <code>OMX_FIRST_PARTY_MCP_SPECS</code> — users add it through standard Codex MCP config or setup wizard output, same as any third-party MCP.</p>
<hr>

<hr>
<h2>17. Codex <code>WebSearchAction</code> protocol (reference)</h2>
<p>When <code>web_search</code> is enabled, Codex serializes actions matching:</p>
<pre><code class="language-rust">// 121_openai-codex/codex-rs/protocol/src/models.rs (lineage reference)
pub enum WebSearchAction {
    Search { query, queries },
    OpenPage { url },
    FindInPage { url, pattern },
    Other,
}
</code></pre>
<p>OMX agents using the researcher role may chain Search → OpenPage conceptually; OMX code does not deserialize these events — the Codex binary handles stream mapping (<code>openai-responses-language-model</code> in codex-rs).</p>
<hr>
<h2>18. Bootstrap MCP entrypoints</h2>
<p><code>getOmxFirstPartySetupMcpServers</code> launches each server as:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// omx-first-party-mcp.ts:90-100
command: process.execPath,
args: [join(pkgRoot, "dist", "mcp", spec.entrypoint)],
startupTimeoutSec: spec.startupTimeoutSec, // 5-10s per server
</code></pre>
<p>Web search latency is therefore <strong>not</strong> subject to OMX MCP startup timeouts — it uses host Responses API instead.</p>
<hr>
<h2>19. Researcher execution loop (prompt excerpt)</h2>
<p>From <code>researcher.md:51-60</code>:</p>
<ol>
<li>Classify request (conceptual / implementation / history / best-practice)</li>
<li>Find official docs or upstream source</li>
<li>Confirm version or date context</li>
<li>Discover doc structure before page fetches</li>
<li>Fetch minimum targeted pages</li>
<li>Add examples after docs baseline</li>
<li>Use OSS references only when docs incomplete (<code>org/repo@sha:path:Lx-Ly</code>)</li>
</ol>
<p>OMX encodes <strong>process</strong>; Codex <code>web_search</code> provides <strong>capability</strong>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>20. Comparison with Copilot CLI (<code>cp</code>)</h2>
<p>Copilot CLI bundles GitHub MCP <code>web_search</code> fallback (<code>151_copilot_cli/deobfuscated/.../C9t</code>). OMX on Codex does not include GitHub MCP web search in its six servers — operators rely on OpenAI hosted search or manual MCP config.</p>
<hr>
<h2>21. Related OMX agents (non-search)</h2>
<p>OMX ships multiple agent prompts under <code>prompts/</code> — <code>explore</code> (repo-local), <code>dependency-expert</code> (package choice), <code>researcher</code> (external docs). Only <strong>researcher</strong> explicitly mandates web search/fetch; misrouting a web query to <code>explore</code> yields repo-only grep — a common operator mistake documented here for corpus parity with <code>003_tool-runtime</code> routing guidance.</p>
<p><strong>Corpus cross-link:</strong> OMX web axis depth intentionally documents <em>absence</em> of first-party search MCPs plus host delegation — same pattern as <code>14_lc_web-search.md</code> (LazyCodex LSP-only) but with researcher prompt and <code>web_search</code> config preservation as positive evidence.</p>

<h2>소스 코드 스니펫</h2>
<h3><code>171_oh-my-codex/README.md</code></h3>
<h2>Quick start</h2>
<h3>Requirements</h3>
<ul>
<li>Node.js 20+</li>
<li>Codex CLI installed, verified with <code>codex --version</code>, and authenticated (Homebrew or npm are both fine; do not reinstall <code>@openai/codex</code> with npm if Homebrew already owns <code>codex</code>)</li>
<li>Codex auth configured and visible in the same shell/profile that will run OMX</li>
<li><code>tmux</code> on macOS/Linux if you want the recommended durable team runtime</li>
<li><code>psmux</code> on native Windows only if you intentionally want the less-supported Windows team path</li>
</ul>
<h3>A good first session</h3>
<p>After install, check both boundaries:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">omx doctor
codex login status
omx exec --skip-git-repo-check -C . "Reply with exactly OMX-EXEC-OK"
</code></pre>
<p><code>omx doctor</code> catches missing OMX files, hooks, and runtime prerequisites. The real smoke test catches auth, profile, and provider/base-URL problems that only appear when Codex performs an actual request.</p>
<p>Launch OMX the recommended way from a git project:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">omx --worktree=feat/task --madmax --high
</code></pre>
<p>On macOS/Linux interactive terminals with <code>tmux</code> available, this starts the
leader in OMX-managed detached tmux by default so the HUD/runtime panes can be
created and recovered. <code>--worktree</code> also moves the launch into a separate git
checkout, which is the safer default when using <code>--madmax</code>. Replace
<code>feat/task</code> with a branch-like name for the task.</p>
<h3>Madmax and worktree launch safety</h3>
<p><code>--madmax</code> is OMX shorthand for Codex
<code>--dangerously-bypass-approvals-and-sandbox</code>. It removes the normal approval and
sandbox guardrails, so only use it in trusted repositories and environments.
<code>--high</code> is shorthand for <code>-c model_reasoning_effort="high"</code>.</p>
<p>When you use <code>--madmax</code> from a git repository, prefer a worktree launch instead
of running directly in the current checkout. For repeatable or concurrent work,
use a named worktree:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">omx --worktree=feature/auth --madmax --high
</code></pre>
<p>If you are outside a git repository, omit <code>--worktree</code>; worktree launches
require Git.</p>
<p>For concurrent <code>--madmax</code> sessions, do <strong>not</strong> run them all in the same
directory. Give each session its own named worktree:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">omx --worktree=feature/auth --madmax --high
omx --worktree=fix/flaky-tests --madmax --high
</code></pre>
<p><code>--worktree</code> / <code>-w</code> with no name creates or reuses a detached launch worktree at
<code>../.omx-worktrees/launch-detached</code>. <code>--worktree=</code>,
<code>--worktree </code>, or <code>-w </code> creates or reuses a named launch worktree
under <code>../.omx-worktrees/</code> and checks out that branch name. OMX consumes
the worktree flag before starting Codex; it is not forwarded to Codex itself.
Treat the unnamed detached form as a one-off convenience: if the source checkout
advances after that worktree is created, a later unnamed launch can fail with
<code>worktree_target_mismatch</code> because <code>launch-detached</code> still points at the old
HEAD. Use a named worktree for repeated work, or remove the old detached
worktree before retrying.
If the target launch worktree is already dirty, OMX warns and launches as-is, so
clean, commit, or stash that worktree before relying on it for isolation.</p>
<p>For <code>omx team</code>, workers already use dedicated worktrees automatically by
default; <code>--worktree</code> on <code>omx team</code> is only a legacy-compatible override.</p>
<p>If you want a one-off launch with no OMX tmux/HUD management, use <code>--direct</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">omx --direct --yolo
</code></pre>
<p>For a persistent shell/profile preference, set an environment policy:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">OMX_LAUNCH_POLICY=direct omx --yolo
</code></pre>
<p>Return to the auto/default behavior with:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">unset OMX_LAUNCH_POLICY
</code></pre>
<p>CLI policy flags win over the environment, and the last CLI policy flag before
<code>--</code> wins:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">OMX_LAUNCH_POLICY=direct omx --tmux --yolo
</code></pre>
<p>Use <code>OMX_LAUNCH_POLICY=direct|tmux|detached-tmux|auto</code>. This iteration only
adds CLI and environment controls; it intentionally does not add a config-file
setting. If you run <code>--direct</code> from inside an existing tmux pane, OMX will not
create HUD splits, enable mouse mode, or wrap extended-key handling, but the
process still runs inside that already-open terminal pane.</p>
<p>Then try the canonical workflow:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">$deep-interview "clarify the authentication change"
$ralplan "approve the safest implementation path"
$ultragoal "turn the approved path into durable Codex goals"
</code></pre>
<p>Use <code>$team</code> when an active Ultragoal story needs coordinated parallel work, or <code>$ralph</code> when one persistent owner should keep pushing to completion without a multi-goal ledger.</p>
<h2>코퍼스 — 015_reverse-engineering/ (심화)</h2>
<h3><code>015_reverse-engineering/00_reverse_evidence_policy.md</code></h3>
<h1>Reverse Engineering Evidence Policy</h1>
<p>이 축은 설치 help parity 문서의 다음 단계다. 기존 <code>00</code>~<code>14</code> 축은 주로 help/config/local-doc 표면을 비교했고, 이 축은 설치된 바이너리와 번들에서 복원 가능한 구조를 따로 기록한다.</p>
<h2>Evidence Levels</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Level</th>
<th>의미</th>
<th>사용할 수 있는 주장</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>installed-help</td>
<td><code>--help</code>, public command output, version output</td>
<td>명령/플래그/공개 subcommand가 존재한다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>safe-local-doc</td>
<td>설치 패키지의 docs, changelog, examples, manifest</td>
<td>문서화된 schema/경로/기능 설명이 있다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>bundle-key</td>
<td>minified bundle에 남은 module key, source path, route name, proto name</td>
<td>내부 모듈/라우터/프로토/컴포넌트가 존재한다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>binary-string</td>
<td>native binary <code>strings</code>, <code>file</code>, <code>otool</code>, <code>codesign</code>, <code>nm</code></td>
<td>crate/package/protocol/tool/evaluator 이름이 embedded되어 있다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>runtime-trace</td>
<td>synthetic project에서 실제 명령을 실행한 결과</td>
<td>동작 semantics, precedence, permission enforcement를 확인했다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>private-artifact-name</td>
<td>비공개 상태 파일의 경로/개수만 관찰</td>
<td>artifact가 존재한다. 내용/schema 주장은 금지</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/015_reverse-engineering/33_source_deobfuscation_inventory.md</code> further separates source-like recovery levels. In this corpus, Cursor reaches preserved module-key recovery, while Grok/Kiro/AGY mostly expose native source-path, handler, protobuf, and runtime-trace evidence. Do not call this "full source recovered" unless a real source map or readable source archive is present.</p>
<h2>Hard Boundary</h2>
<p>역분석의 목적은 제품 구조 복원이지 사용자 상태 추출이 아니다. 다음은 내용 읽기 금지다.</p>
<ul>
<li>auth/token/cookie/credential/login data</li>
<li>raw transcript, chat history, conversation DB/PB</li>
<li>logs and terminal captures</li>
<li>browser profile state, local storage, IndexedDB, session storage</li>
<li>memory/goal runtime stores</li>
<li>screenshots and browser recordings</li>
<li>private <code>mcp.json</code>, settings, config values unless explicitly redacted</li>
</ul>
<p>비공개 artifact는 “존재한다”까지만 쓴다. 필드/schema/content 주장은 public docs, source/bundle evidence, sanitized fixture, synthetic runtime trace가 있을 때만 쓴다.</p>
<h2>Installed CLI version pin (2026-06-27)</h2>

<ul>
<li><code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/015_reverse-engineering/36_installed_cli_version_manifest.md</code></li>
</ul>
<p>WP5 trace shards (<code>38</code>–<code>41</code>) extend hubs without changing evidence-level definitions above.</p>

<h2>Reading Rule For Existing Docs</h2>
<p>When a <code>00</code>~<code>14</code> page says “없음” or “지원하지 않음”, interpret it as “installed help에서 노출되지 않음” unless this <code>15_reverse-engineering</code> axis confirms absence from bundle/binary evidence too.</p>
<p>When a page states runtime semantics from config/cache observation, this axis upgrades or downgrades the claim:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>bundle-key</code> or <code>binary-string</code> confirms a module exists.</li>
<li><code>runtime-trace</code> is still required for exact precedence, scheduling, isolation, merge, and permission behavior.</li>
</ul>

<h2>000/00_grand_synthesis.md (발췌)</h2>
<h1>GRAND SYNTHESIS — 5개 코딩 에이전트 × 13개 차원 최종 종합 분석</h1>
<p>이 문서는 Codex, Aider, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Claude Code를 13개 아키텍처 차원에서 동시에 비교한 캡스톤 문서다.
개별 비교 문서의 결론을 단순 재배열하지 않고, 서로 다른 설계 철학이 어떤 제품 전략으로 수렴하는지까지 읽어내는 것을 목표로 한다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A[5개 에이전트 개요] --> B[13개 차원 비교]
    B --> C[공통 패턴 추출]
    B --> D[핵심 차별점 추출]
    C --> E[기술 선택 시사점]
    D --> E
    E --> F[미래 전망과 설계 교훈]
</code></pre>
<h2>1. 개요</h2>
<h3>이 문서의 목적</h3>
<p>이 문서의 목적은 5개 에이전트를 한 번에 조망할 수 있는 상위 레퍼런스를 만드는 것이다.
개별 문서는 특정 축의 우열을 설명하지만, 실제 제품 선택은 언제나 여러 축의 동시 판단을 요구한다.
따라서 여기서는 TUI, prompt, tool, skill, subagent, app-server, sandbox, config, MCP, memory, plugin, guardian, 그리고 잔여 교차 관심사를 하나의 프레임으로 다시 묶는다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[00_ai_overview]], [[00_ge_overview]], [[00_oc_overview]], [[00_cc_overview]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>분석 범위</h3>
<p>범위는 5개 에이전트와 13개 차원이다.
에이전트는 Codex, Aider, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Claude Code다.
차원은 TUI, Prompt/Context, Tool Runtime, Skill, Subagents, App-Server Surface, Sandbox, Config, MCP, Memory, Plugin, Guardian, 잔여 교차 관심사(Git/VCS, 모델 라우팅, 에러 처리, 텔레메트리, IDE 통합, 패키징, 테스트, 인증, 멀티모달, 이벤트 시스템, 피처 플래그, 국제화)다.
App-Server 축은 비교 문서 자체가 Codex·Gemini CLI·OpenCode 중심으로 작성되어 있으므로 Aider와 Claude Code는 “의도적 부재”까지 함께 해석한다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]], [[004_skill-system/00_skill]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]], [[006_app-server-client-surfaces/00_surface]], [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[008_config-system/00_config]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]], [[010_memory-pipeline/00_memory]], [[011_plugin-system/00_plugin]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]], [[013_etc/00_etc]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>분석 방법론</h3>
<p>첫째, 각 에이전트 개요 문서에서 기술 스택, 패키지 구조, 핵심 철학을 추출했다.
둘째, 13개 비교 문서에서 축별 우위와 결손, 스카우팅 점수, 디자인 패턴을 수집했다.
셋째, 같은 에이전트가 여러 축에서 반복적으로 보이는 패턴을 묶어 장기 전략으로 재해석했다.
넷째, 단일 승자를 찾기보다 “어떤 상황에서 어떤 설계가 더 설득력 있는가”를 기준으로 실무 추천안을 도출했다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[00_ai_overview]], [[00_ge_overview]], [[00_oc_overview]], [[00_cc_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>이 문서를 읽는 방법</h3>
<p>제품 선택이 목적이면 3장, 7장, 8장을 먼저 보는 것이 좋다.
포크나 재구현이 목적이면 2장, 5장, 6장, 9장을 먼저 보는 것이 좋다.
보안 검토가 목적이면 3장, 4장, 8장, 9장을 함께 읽는 편이 낫다.
마지막 부록은 문서 인덱스 역할을 하므로 세부 원문으로 돌아갈 때 사용하면 된다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]], [[011_plugin-system/00_plugin]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]]</li>
</ul>

<h3>Codex</h3>
<ul>
<li>정체성: 엔진을 층으로 분리하고, prompt·tool·skill·subagent·MCP를 제어면(control plane)으로 다룬다.</li>
<li>기술 스택: Rust + TypeScript + React/Ink + app-server protocol</li>
<li>핵심 차별점: 가장 분해 가능한 core engine, 가장 강한 terminal-native orchestration, 가장 균형 잡힌 sandbox/MCP 결합.</li>
<li>실무에서 강한 상황: 보안, 오케스트레이션, 포크 가능한 core engine이 중요한 팀</li>
<li>재구현 관점 한 줄 평: requirements 제약 채널과 prompt fragment provenance를 분리한 구조.</li>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]], [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>Aider</h3>
<ul>
<li>정체성: 도구 플랫폼보다 코드 편집 루프에 집중한다. 모델을 좋은 editor로 만드는 쪽에 최적화한다.</li>
<li>기술 스택: Python + prompt_toolkit + rich + tree-sitter + Git</li>
<li>핵심 차별점: RepoMap, edit 전략 다양성, git auto-com</li>
</ul>
